	name = EU_parl_PG_party_0_support
	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				has_global_flag = global.PG_party_0_support
			}
		}
		localization_key = EU_parl_PG_party_0_support_loc_key
	}
}
